## Page 48

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">内置函数 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">abs</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 返回整数和浮点数的绝对值，以及复数的模。为了保持一</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">致性，我们的 API 也使用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">abs</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 函数计算向量的模。</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">&gt;&gt;&gt; v = Vector(3, 4) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">&gt;&gt;&gt; abs(v) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">5.0</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">还可以实现 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">*</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 运算符，计算向量的标量积（即一个向量乘以一个数，得</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">到一个方向相同、模为一定倍数的新向量）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">&gt;&gt;&gt; v * 3 </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">Vector(9, 12) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">&gt;&gt;&gt; abs(v * 3) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">15.0</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">示例 1-2 使用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__abs__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__add__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__mul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 等特</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">殊方法为 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 类实现这几种运算。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">示例</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">1-2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">　一个简单的二维向量类</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">&quot;&quot;&quot; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">vector2d.py</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">：一个简单的类，演示一些特殊方法</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">只是演示，一些问题做简化处理。缺少错误处理，尤其是</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">__add__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">__mul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">方法。</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">本书后文还会扩充这个示例。</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">加法</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">:: </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    &gt;&gt;&gt; v1 = Vector(2, 4) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    &gt;&gt;&gt; v2 = Vector(2, 1) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    &gt;&gt;&gt; v1 + v2 </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    Vector(4, 5) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">绝对值</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">:: </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    &gt;&gt;&gt; v = Vector(3, 4) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    &gt;&gt;&gt; abs(v) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    5.0 </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">标量积</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">:: </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    &gt;&gt;&gt; v * 3 </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    Vector(9, 12) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    &gt;&gt;&gt; abs(v * 3) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    15.0 </span>

## Page 49

<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">&quot;&quot;&quot; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">import math </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">class Vector: </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    def __init__(self, x=0, y=0): </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        self.x = x </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        self.y = y </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    def __repr__(self): </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        return f&#x27;Vector({self.x!r}, {self.y!r})&#x27; </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    def __abs__(self): </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        return math.hypot(self.x, self.y) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    def __bool__(self): </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        return bool(abs(self)) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    def __add__(self, other): </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        x = self.x + other.x </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        y = self.y + other.y </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        return Vector(x, y) </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    def __mul__(self, scalar): </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        return Vector(self.x * scalar, self.y * scalar)</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">除了我们熟悉的 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__init__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法，这个类还实现了另外 5 个特殊方</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">法。注意，这些方法在类内部，或者在前面的 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">doctest</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 中都没有直接</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">调用。正如前文所说，多数特殊方法最常被 Python 解释器调用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">示例 1-2 实现了 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">+</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">*</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 两个运算符，展示了 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__add__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__mul__</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">方法的基本用法。这两个方法创建并返回一个新 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 实例，没有修</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">改运算对象，只是读取 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">self</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 或 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">other</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">。这是中缀运算符的预期行</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">为，即创建新对象，不修改运算对象。这一点会在第 16 章详谈。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">　按照示例 1-2 中的实现，一个 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 对象可以乘以一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">数，但是一个数不能乘以一个 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 对象，这违背了标量积的交</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">换律。这个问题在第 16 章会使用特殊方法 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__rmul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 解决。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">接下来的几节讨论 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 类的其他特殊方法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">1.3.2</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">　</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">字符串表示形式</span>

![](./流畅的 Python (Luciano Ramalho) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p049_img01.png)

---

## Page 50

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">特殊方法 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 供内置函数 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">repr</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 调用，获取对象的字符串表示</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">形式。如未定义 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法，</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 实例在 Python 控制台中</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">显示为 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">&lt;Vector object at 0x10e100070&gt;</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 形式。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">交互式控制台和调试器在表达式求值结果上调用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">repr</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 函数，处理方式</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">与使用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">%</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 运算符处理经典格式化方式中的 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">%r</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 占位符，以及使用</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">str.format</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法处理新字符串格式化句法中的 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">!r</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 转换字段一样。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">注意，</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 类 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法中的 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">f</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 字符串使用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">!r</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 以标准的表</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">示形式显示属性。这样做比较好，因为 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector(1, 2)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector(&#x27;1&#x27;, &#x27;2&#x27;)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 之间是有区别的，后者在这个示例中不可用，因</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">为构造函数接受的参数是数值而不是字符串。</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法返回的字符串应当没有歧义，如果可能，最好与源码保</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">持一致，方便重新创建所表示的对象。鉴于此，我们才以类似构造函数</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">的形式（例如 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector(3, 4)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">）返回 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 对象的字符串表示形</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">式。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">与此形成对照的是，</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__str__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法由内置函数 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">str()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 调用，在背后供</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">print</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 函数使用，返回对终端用户友好的字符串。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">有时，</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法返回的字符串足够友好，无须再定义 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__str__</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">方法，因为继承自 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">object</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 类的实现最终会调用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法。本</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">书中有几个示例定义了 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__str__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法，例如示例 5-2。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">　如果你熟悉的编程语言使用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">toString</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法，那么你可能习</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">惯实现 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__str__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法而不是 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法。在 Python 中，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">如果必须二选一的话，请选择 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Stack Overflow 网站中有一个问题，“What is the difference</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">between </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__str__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> and </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">?”，Python 专家 Alex</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Martelli 和 Martijn Pieters 对此做出了详尽解答。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">1.3.3</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">　</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">自定义类型的布尔值</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Python 有一个 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">bool</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 类型，在需要布尔值的地方处理对象，例如 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">if</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">或 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">while</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 语句的条件表达式，或者 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">and</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">or</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">not</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 的运算对象。为</span>

![](./流畅的 Python (Luciano Ramalho) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p050_img01.png)

---

## Page 51

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">了确定 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">x</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 表示的值为</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">真</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">或为</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">假</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">，Python 调用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">bool(x)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">，返回 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">True</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">或 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">False</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">默认情况下，用户定义类的实例都是真值，除非实现了 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__bool__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 或</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__len__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法。简单来说，</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">bool(x)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 调用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">x.__bool__()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">，以后者</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">返回的结果为准。如果没有实现 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__bool__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法，则 Python 尝试调用</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">x.__len__()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">；如果该方法返回零值，则 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">bool</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 函数返回 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">False</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">，否</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">则返回 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">True</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">我们实现的 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__bool__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法没用到什么高深的理论，如果向量的模为</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">零，则返回 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">False</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">，否则返回 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">True</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">。我们使用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">bool(abs(self))</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">把向量的模转换成布尔值，因为 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__bool__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法必须返回一个布尔值。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">在 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__bool__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法外部，很少需要显式调用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">bool()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">，因为任何对象</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">都可在布尔值上下文中使用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">注意，这个 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__bool__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 特殊方法遵守 Python 标准库文档中“Built-in</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Types”一章里定义的真值测试规则。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">　</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Vector.__bool__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法也可以像下面这样简单定义。</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">    def __bool__(self): </span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">        return bool(self.x or self.y)</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">这样定义虽然不易读懂，但是不用经过 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">abs</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__abs__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 处理，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">也无须计算平方和平方根。使用 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">bool</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 显式转换是有必要的，因为</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__bool__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法必须返回一个布尔值。</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">or</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 返回两个操作数的其中</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">一个，而且原封不动：如果 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">x</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 是真值，则 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">x or y</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 的求值结果为</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">x</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">，否则为 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">y</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">，无论 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">y</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 是真是假。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">1.3.4</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">　</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">容器</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:18.57pt;color:#000000">API</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Python 语言中基本容器类型的接口如图 1-2 所示。图中所有的类都是</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">抽象基类</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">。抽象基类和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">collections.abc</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 模块将在第 13 章讨论。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">本节简要说明 Python 中最重要的容器接口，纵览容器类型对特殊方法</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">的使用情况。</span>

![](./流畅的 Python (Luciano Ramalho) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p051_img01.png)

---

## Page 52

<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">图</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">1-2：基本容器类型的</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">UML</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">类图。以斜体显示的方法名称表示抽象</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">方法，必须由具体子类（例如</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPS-BoldMT';font-size:14.38pt;font-weight:bold;color:#000000">list</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPS-BoldMT';font-size:14.38pt;font-weight:bold;color:#000000">dict</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">）实现。其他方法有具体</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">实现，子类可以直接继承</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">顶部 3 个抽象基类均只有一个特殊方法。抽象基类 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Collection</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">（Python 3.6 新增）统一了这 3 个基本接口，每一个容器类型均应实</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">现如下事项：</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Iterable</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 要支持 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">for</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">、拆包和其他迭代方式；</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Sized</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 要支持内置函数 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">len</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">；</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Container</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 要支持 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">in</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 运算符。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Python 不强制要求具体类继承这些抽象基类中的任何一个。只要实现了</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__len__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 方法，就说明那个类满足 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Sized</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 接口。</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Collection</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 有 3 个十分重要的专用接口：</span>

![](./流畅的 Python (Luciano Ramalho) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p052_img01.png)

## Page 53

<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Sequence</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 规范 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">str</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 等内置类型的接口；</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Mapping</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 被 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">dict</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">collections.defaultdict</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 等实现；</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Set</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 是 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">set</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">frozenset</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 两个内置类型的接口。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">只有 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Sequence</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 实现了 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Reversible</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">，因为序列要支持以任意顺序排</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">列内容，而 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Mapping</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Set</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 不需要。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">　自 Python 3.7 开始，</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">dict</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 类型正式“有顺序”了，不过只</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">是保留键的插入顺序。你不能随意重新排列 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">dict</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 中的键。</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">Set</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 抽象基类中的所有特殊方法实现的都是中缀运算符。例如，</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">a &amp; b</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">计算集合 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">a</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">b</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 的交集，该运算符由 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__and__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 特殊方法实现。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">接下来的两章会详细说明标准库中的序列、映射和集合。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">接下来按大类介绍 Python 数据模型定义的特殊方法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:23.96pt;color:#000000">1.4</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:23.96pt;color:#000000">　</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:23.96pt;color:#000000">特殊方法概述</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">《Python 语言参考手册》中的第 3 章列出了 80 多个特殊方法名称，</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">其中一半以上用于实现算术运算符、按位运算符和比较运算符。下面几</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">张表格概述了这些可用的特殊方法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">表 1-1 不包含实现中缀运算符和核心数学函数（例如 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">abs</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">）的特殊方</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">法。这里列出的多数特殊方法本书中有所讨论，包括新增的几个，比如</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__anext__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">（Python 3.5 新增）等异步特殊方法，以及为类定义钩子</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">的 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__init_subclass__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">（Python 3.6 新增）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">表</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">1-1：特殊方法名称（不含运算符）</span>

<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">分类</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">方法名称</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">字符串（字节）表示</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">形式</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__repr__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__str__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__format__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__bytes__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__fspath__</span>

<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__mro_entries__</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">中缀运算符和数字运算符由表 1-2 中的特殊方法提供支持。其中，</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__matmul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__rmatmul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 和 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">__imatmul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 是 Python 3.5 新增</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">的，用于实现矩阵乘法中缀运算符 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">@</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">（见第 16 章）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">表</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">1-2：运算符的符号和背后的特殊方法</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">反向算</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">术运算</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">符</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">+</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">-</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">*</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">/</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">//</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">%</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">@</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">divmod()</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">round()</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">**</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">pow()</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__add__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__sub__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__mul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__truediv__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__floordiv__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__mod__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__matmul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__divmod__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__round__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__pow__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__radd__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rsub__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rmul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rtruediv__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rfloordiv__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rmod__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rmatmul__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rdivmod__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rpow__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__iadd__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__isub__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__imul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__itruediv__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__ifloordiv__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__imod__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__imatmul__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__ipow__</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">（交换算术运算符的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">操作数）</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">增量赋</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">值算术</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">运算符</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">+=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">-=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">*=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">/=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">//=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">%=</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">@=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">**=</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">按位运</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">算符</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">&amp;</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">|</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">^</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">&lt;&lt;</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">&gt;&gt;</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">~</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__and__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__or__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__xor__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__lshift__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rshift__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__invert__</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">反向按</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">位运算</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">符</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">（交换按位运算符的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">操作数）</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rand__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__ror__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rxor__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rlshift__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__rrshift__</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">增量赋</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">值按位</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000">运算符</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">&amp;=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">|=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">^=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">&lt;&lt;=</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">&gt;&gt;=</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__iand__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__ior__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__ixor__</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.78pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__ilshift__</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">__irshift__</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">　如果第一个操作数对应的特殊方法不可用，则 Python 在第二</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">个操作数上调用反向运算符对应的特殊方法。增量赋值是结合了变</span>

## Page 56

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">量赋值功能的中缀运算符的简写形式，例如 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">a += b</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">第 16 章会详细说明反向运算符和增量赋值。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:23.96pt;color:#000000">1.5</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:23.96pt;color:#000000">　</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPS-BoldMT';font-size:23.96pt;font-weight:bold;color:#000000">len</span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:23.96pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'Unnamed-T3';font-size:23.96pt;color:#000000">为什么不是方法</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">这个问题我在 2013 年问过核心开发人员 Raymond Hettinger，他在回</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">答时引用了《Python 之禅》中的一句话，道出了玄机：“实用胜过纯</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">粹。”1.3 节说过，当 </span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">x</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 是内置类型的实例时，</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">len(x)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000"> 运行速度非常</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">快。计算 CPython 内置对象的长度时不调用任何方法，而是直接读取 C</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">语言结构体中的字段。获取容器中的项数是一项常见操作，</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">str</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">list</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'CourierNewPSMT';font-size:14.38pt;color:#000000">memoryview</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:14.38pt;co
